# Morale  
> Shows your general mood. Affects your immune system and can help trigger depressive and manic states at the extremes.  
> "Your morale represents how well you feel at a given moment.<br><br>At low levels your morale can compromise your <b>Immune System</b>  
  
<div style="font-size:1.2em"><b>Base Value: </b> 0 </div>  
<div style="font-size:1.2em"><b>Value Range: </b> -350 ~ 350 </div>  
<div style="font-size:1.2em"><b>Base Rate: </b> - </div>  
<div style="font-size:1.2em"><b>Staleness: </b>Staleness multiplier 50% in <font data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="96TP">1d</font>(stack:2) </div>
